This was the dash log and stringify'ed JSON of the npc array for a long and sentimental run.
First run with a working death function and enough males to keep the colony going so I could see full life cycle.
Sweet Stuart and Kimberlee, teenage lovers who saw 80 years of trials and tribulations, love and betrayal.
Cecilia, who lived to 117!
Kimberlee and Elliana, those minxes who slept with half the colony.
Kimberlee, who had 13 children and 9 grandchildren at her death.
This 'game' has potential, I think.
